",["$","strong",null,{"children":"Mastery"}]," - Deep system understanding and optimization (distinct from Challenge: not just overcoming but understanding deeply)\n10. 32:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Five Pacing Patterns:"}]}]
33:["$","ol",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Attrition"}]," - Gradual pressure buildup, slow resource depletion, strategic decisions compound"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Episodic"}]," - Self-contained scenes, fast recovery, fresh start each encounter"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Wave"}]," - Cyclical intensity (build → peak → relief → repeat), multiple cycles per session"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Continuous"}]," - Steady state, no clear breaks, real-time or seamless flow"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Punctuated"}]," - Long calm periods interrupted by sudden intense moments"]}],"\n"]}]
34:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Key Measurables:"}]}]

4b:["$","ol",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":["\n",["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Consumable"}]," - Depletes with use, gone when spent"]}],"\n",["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Examples: HP, spell slots, gold, ammunition"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Creates: Scarcity pressure, strategic allocation"}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":["\n",["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Buffer"}]," - 60:["$","h3",null,{"className":"flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2","id":"cognitive-load-framework","children":[["$","a",null,{"data-card":"","href":"#cognitive-load-framework","className":"peer","children":"Cognitive Load Framework"}],["$","svg",null,{"xmlns":"http://www.w3.org/2000/svg","width":24,"height":24,"viewBox":"0 0 24 24","fill":"none","stroke":"currentColor","strokeWidth":2,"strokeLinecap":"round","strokeLinejoin":"round","className":"lucide size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100","aria-label":"Link to section","children":[[["$","path","1cjeqo",{"d":"M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"}],["$","path","19qd67",{"d":"M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"}]],"$undefined"]}]]}]
61:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Core Insight:"}]," Cognitive load is a CONSTRAINT (external to game state), not a resource (internal game mechanic)."]}]
62:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Critical Distinction:"}]}]
63:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Resources:"}]," In-game entities (HP, gold, spell slots) - can be spent, recovered, traded"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Cognitive Load:"}]," Player mental capacity - cannot be \"spent\" or \"recovered\" within game mechanics"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Tools for resource design (scarcity, recovery) don't apply to cognitive load"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Must use different strategies: offloading, simplification, support systems"}],"\n"]}]
64:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Seven Load Types:"}]}]
65:["$","ol",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Simultaneity Load"}]," - Tracking multiple things at once (real-time pressure, parallel threads)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Decision Load"}]," - Evaluating options and making choices (how many options? how deep?)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Memory/Knowledge Load"}]," - Recalling information (rules, lore, previous state)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Tracking Load"}]," - Monitoring ongoing game state (positions, resources, conditions)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Calculation Load"}]," - Mathematical processing and computation (formulas, probabilities)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Pattern Recognition Load"}]," - Learning through repeated experience (boss patterns, strategic meta)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Social/Communication Load"}]," - Interpersonal coordination, deception, negotiation, reputation"]}],"\n"]}]
66:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Load-Aesthetic Relationships:"}]}]
67:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Challenge aesthetic"}]," → HIGH decision/pattern load (but must be conquerable)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Fellowship aesthetic"}]," → LOW mechanical load, HIGH social load (brainspace for socializing)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Narrative aesthetic"}]," → LOW calculation load (math breaks immersion)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Mastery aesthetic"}]," → HIGH load that DECREASES with practice (front-loaded difficulty)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Discovery aesthetic"}]," → Variable load (tolerates \"messy\" complexity for exploration)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Submission aesthetic"}]," → VERY LOW load (relaxation, not mental effort)"]}],"\n"]}]
68:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Player Type Preferences (Bartle + Load):"}]}]
69:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Achievers"}]," → Want conquerable high load (optimization, mastery through effort)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Explorers"}]," → Tolerate messy load (discovery-driven, depth over clarity)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Socializers"}]," → Prefer low mechanical load (brainspace for social interaction)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Killers"}]," → Embrace competitive load (management as competitive advantage)"]}],"\n"]}]
6a:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Investment Changes Load Over Time:"}]}]
6b:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Load Reduction Pattern"}]," (Dark Souls): Practice internalizes patterns → less cognitive load"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Load Revelation Pattern"}]," (StarCraft): Basics automate → notice deeper complexity"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Load Independence Pattern"}]," (Cookie Clicker): Time passes, load stays constant"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Load Creep Pattern"}]," (Trading Card Games): Complexity accumulates over game's lifecycle"]}],"\n"]}]
6c:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Core Design Principles:"}]}]

82:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Cognitive Load Terms"}]," (always use specific types):"]}]
83:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"The Seven Load Types (Mandatory - Never Substitute):"}]}]
84:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Simultaneity load\" (not \"multitasking,\" \"parallel processing,\" \"concurrent demands\")"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Decision load\" (not \"choice complexity,\" \"option overload,\" \"decision space\")"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Memory load\" or \"Knowledge load\" (not \"recall burden,\" \"knowledge requirements,\" \"memorization\")"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Tracking load\" (not \"state management,\" \"bookkeeping,\" \"monitoring burden\")"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Calculation load\" (not \"math burden,\" \"computational complexity,\" \"arithmetic overhead\")"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Pattern recognition load\" (not \"learning curve,\" \"skill development,\" \"mastery requirement\")"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Social load\" or \"Communication load\" (not \"coordination overhead,\" \"social complexity\")"}],"\n"]}]
85:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Load Management Terms:"}]}]
86:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Support load\" (not \"reduce burden,\" \"help players\") - when providing tools/UI/externalization"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Remove load\" (not \"simplify,\" \"dumb down\") - when eliminating unnecessary complexity"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Offload\" (not \"delegate,\" \"transfer\") - when moving load to GM/computer/LLM"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Externalize\" (not \"document,\" \"write down\") - when moving memory to physical/digital aids"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Necessary load\" (not \"good complexity\") - load that serves experience"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Unnecessary load\" (not \"bad complexity,\" \"friction\") - load that obstructs experience"}],"\n"]}]
87:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Resource-Related Terms (From Resource Management Chapter):"}]}]
88:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Buffer resource\" (not \"protective resource,\" \"shield resource\") - Blades stress-type resources"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Composition resource\" (not \"build resource,\" \"synergy resource\") - deck-building type resources"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Consumable resource\" (not \"spent resource,\" \"used-up resource\") - depletes with use"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Accumulation resource\" (not \"progression resource,\" \"growth resource\") - collects over time"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Capacity resource\" (not \"limit resource,\" \"slot resource\") - constrains what's possible"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Recovery pattern\" (not \"regeneration,\" \"refresh rate,\" \"restoration\") - how resources replenish"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Possession effect\" (not \"having experience,\" \"ownership feeling\") - psychological state from owning"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Greed behavior\" (not \"hoarding,\" \"accumulation syndrome\") - psychological pattern"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"FOMO\" (not \"anxiety,\" \"scarcity stress\") - Fear of Missing Out, only for time-limited content"}],"\n"]}]
89:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Resource Recovery Terms:"}]}]
8a:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Fast recovery\" (not \"quick refresh,\" \"instant regen\") - seconds to minutes"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Moderate recovery\" (not \"medium refresh\") - per-encounter, per-scene"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Slow recovery\" (not \"long cooldown\") - per-session, per-campaign"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"No recovery\" (not \"permanent loss\" in adjective form) - never recovers"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Mixed recovery\" (not \"variable recovery\") - different rates for different resources"}],"\n"]}]
8b:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Critical Distinctions:"}]}]
8c:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Cognitive load is a constraint\" (not \"resource,\" \"currency,\" \"cost\")"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Players have cognitive capacity\" (not \"manage cognitive load,\" \"spend attention\")"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Designers accommodate load\" (not \"players control load,\" \"balance complexity\")"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"\"Resource\" vs. \"Constraint\""}]," (CRITICAL - never confuse these):","\n",["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Resource: In-game entity (HP, gold, stress) - tracked by system, can be spent/recovered/traded"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Constraint: External limitation (cognitive load, time, attention) - player capacity, not game mechanic"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"NEVER say: \"Attention is a resource\" or \"Cognitive load is a resource\""}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"ALWAYS say: \"Attention is a constraint\" or \"Cognitive load is a design constraint\""}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Rationale: Tools for resource design (scarcity, recovery) don't apply to constraints"}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}]
8d:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Context-Specific:"}]}]
8e:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Load profile\" (not \"complexity level,\" \"difficulty curve\") - overall cognitive demand pattern"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Load mismatch\" (not \"complexity problem,\" \"difficulty issue\") - when load doesn't serve aesthetic"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"\"Load appropriate\" (not \"well-designed,\" \"balanced\") - when load matches intended experience"}],"\n"]}]

f1:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"Standard anti-pattern codes for consistent reference across chapters:"}]}]
f2:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"AP-RM-1: Critical Path Resources"}]}]
f3:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Problem: Gating progress-critical elements behind depletable/missable resources"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Example: D&D investigation (roll to find clues → can fail → investigation stalls)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Why it fails: Creates dead stops, not interesting challenges"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Solution: Core elements automatic, optional elements cost resources (Gumshoe model)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Recognition: \"If players run out of X, can game continue interestingly?\" If NO → Don't make it depletable"}],"\n"]}]
f4:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"AP-RM-2: System Selection Error"}]}]
f5:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Problem: Using resource system designed for different aesthetic"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Example: D&D (combat-focused) for mystery investigation (interpretation-focused)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Why it fails: Mechanics fight against intended experience"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Solution: Choose system that serves aesthetic, or heavily modify"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Recognition: \"What is this system optimized for? Does it match my goal?\""}],"\n"]}]
f6:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"AP-RM-3: Meaningless Accumulation"}]}]
f7:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Problem: Resources accumulate without creating decisions"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Example: Grinding for levels (time investment, not skill expression)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Why it fails: Reduces Challenge to Submission (mindless activity)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Solution: Tie accumulation to choices, not just time"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Recognition: \"Could a bot do this?\" If YES → Problem"}],"\n"]}]
f8:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"AP-RM-4: Resource Starvation"}]}]
f9:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Problem: Players can't afford to use core mechanics"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Example: Wizard with 2 spell slots saves them, never casts"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Why it fails: Core fantasy inaccessible, reduces to basic actions"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Solution: Increase abundance or add free baseline version (cantrips)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Recognition: Playtest shows players hoarding and never using abilities"}],"\n"]}]
fa:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"AP-RM-5: Unintended Grinding"}]}]
fb:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Problem: Optimal play requires repetitive resource farming"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Example: Need gold for potions → farm easy enemies repeatedly"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Why it fails: Interrupts pacing, boring, feels necessary"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Solution: Make farming impossible/inefficient, make resources abundant, or make farming fun"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Recognition: \"What's optimal way to get X?\" If answer is \"repeat boring thing\" → Problem"}],"\n"]}]
fc:["$","p",null,{"children":["$","strong",null,{"children":"AP-RM-6: Manipulative FOMO"}]}]
fd:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Problem: Creating anxiety through time-limited content for retention metrics"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Example: Daily quest treadmills with exclusive rewards"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Why it fails: Engagement through anxiety, not enjoyment; game becomes job"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Solution: Make events recurring, remove exclusive rewards, no \"use it or lose it\" pressure"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Recognition: \"Does missing this create anxiety or disappointment?\" Anxiety → Manipulative"}],"\n"]}]
